                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">صَبَرَهُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bi" lang="ar">صَبِرَ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, M, A, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">صَبْرٌ</foreign>, (M, K,) <hi rend="ital">He confined him; held him in custody; detained, retained, restrained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">withheld, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi> (S, M, A, K;) <foreign lang="ar">عَنْهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">from it.</hi> (M, A, K.) [Accord. to a copy of the A,   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-1" target="صبّرهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23661"/></foreign> signifies the same; but this may be a mistranscription. Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرْتُ نَفْسِى</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I restrained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">withheld, myself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">my soul;</hi> (S, Mgh;) <foreign lang="ar">عَلَى كَذَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">to endure such a thing</hi>]. (Mgh.) 'Antarah says, mentioning a battle in which he was engaged, <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">فَصَبَرْتُ عَارِفَةً لِذٰلِكَ حُرَّةً</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">تَرْسُوا إِذَا نَفْسُ الجَبَانِ تَطَلَّعُ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> meaning <foreign lang="ar">حَبَسْتُ نَفْسًا صَابِرَةً</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">And I restrained thereat a soul patient</hi> and <hi rend="ital">ingenuous, that is firm when the soul of the coward yearns:</hi> the last word (for <foreign lang="ar">تَتَطَلَّعُ</foreign>) I have here rendered on the supposition that the poet describes the soul of the coward as one that is yearning for home]. (S.) [And hence,] <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرَ</foreign> is also used intransitively: (Msb:) [or as a trans. verb of which the objective complement, namely, <foreign lang="ar">نَفْسَهُ</foreign>, is understood:] you say, <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرَ</foreign>, aor. and inf. n. as above, (S, M, Msb, K,) <hi rend="ital">He was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became patient,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">enduring; contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">جَزِعَ</foreign>: (M, K:) or <hi rend="ital">he restrained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">withheld, himself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">his soul, from impatience:</hi> (S, Msb:) or <hi rend="ital">he restrained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">withheld, himself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">his soul, from impatience, and his tongue from complaint, and his members from broil:</hi> or, accord. to Dhu-n-Noon, <hi rend="ital">he shunned acts of opposition, and was calm in suffering the pangs of afflictions, and made a show of competence in a state of protracted poverty in places where the means of subsistence were found:</hi> or, as some say, <hi rend="ital">he endured trial,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">affliction, with good manners:</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he was contented in trial,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">affliction, without show of complaint:</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he constrained himself to attempt things that he disliked:</hi> or, accord. to 'Amr Ibn-'Othmán, <hi rend="ital">he maintained constancy with God, and received his trials with an unstraitened mind:</hi> or, accord. to El-Khowwás, <hi rend="ital">he steadily adhered to the statutes of the Kur-án and the Sunneh:</hi> or, as some say, <hi rend="ital">he was content to perish for gaining the approval of him whom he loved:</hi> or, accord. to El-Hareeree, <hi rend="ital">he made no difference between a state of ease, comfort, and affluence, and a state of affliction; preserving calmness of mind in both states:</hi> (B:) and you also say   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-2" target="اِصْطَبَرَ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23665"/></foreign>, (S, M, Msb, K,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-3" target="اِصَّبَرَ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (S, M, K, TA, [in the CK, erroneously, <foreign lang="ar">اصْبَرَّ</foreign>,]) <pb n="1644"/> changing the <foreign lang="ar">ط</foreign> into <foreign lang="ar">ص</foreign>, but not <foreign lang="ar">اِطَّبَرَ</foreign>, for <foreign lang="ar">ص</foreign> is not to be incorporated into <foreign lang="ar">ط</foreign>; (S;) and likewise   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-4" target="تصبّر" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23660"/></foreign>; (M, K;) both syn. with <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرَ</foreign>; (M;) or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-5" target="تصبّر" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23660"/></foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he constrained himself to be patient;</hi> (S, TA;) [or <hi rend="ital">he took patience:</hi> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-6" target="اصطبر" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, <hi rend="ital">he acquired patience;</hi> and <hi rend="ital">he was tried with patience:</hi> see <foreign lang="ar">صَابِرٌ</foreign>.] One says, <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرَ فُلَانٌ عِنْدَ المُصِيبَةِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Such a one was patient on the occasion of affliction.</hi> (S.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرْتُ عَلَى مَا أَكْرَهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I was patient of,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I endured with patience,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">bore with, what I dislike</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَبَرْتُ عَمَّا أُحِبُّ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I endured with patience the withholding of myself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the being debarred, from what I love,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">like;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I was patient of the loss,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">want, of what I love,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">like</hi>]: (A:) and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23660-7" target="تَصَبَّرْتُ" n="7" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>عَنْهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I constrained myself to endure with patience the withholding myself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the being debarred, from it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">him;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I constrained myself to be patient of the loss,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">want, of it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">him</hi>]. (L, voce <foreign lang="ar">تَجَلَّدَ</foreign>.) And
